9_CD ._. 1_CD ._. 1_LS The_DT objective_NN of_IN chronic_JJ aquatic_JJ toxicity_NN tests_NNS with_IN

"_'' no-effect_JJ concentration_NN "_'' of_IN these_DT substances_NNS ._. For_IN practical_JJ

when_WRB compared_VBN to_TO the_DT controls_NNS ._. The_DT terms_NNS currently_RB used_VBN to_TO define_VB

9_CD ._. 1_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 1_CD

9_CD ._. 3_CD ._. 1_LS HYPOTHESIS_NNP TESTS_NNS
9_CD ._. 3_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 1_CD When_WRB hypothesis_NNS tests_NNS are_VBP used_VBN to_TO analyze_VB toxicity_NN test_NN
data_NNS ,_, it_PRP is_VBZ not_RB possible_JJ to_TO express_VB precision_NN in_IN terms_NNS of_IN a_DT

0_CD ._. 5_CD dilution_NN factor_NN (_( two-fold_JJ difference_NN between_IN adjacent_JJ

9_CD ._. 3_CD ._. 2_LS POINT_NNP ESTIMATION_NNP TECHNIQUES_NNP

It_PRP should_MD be_VB noted_VBN that_DT software_NN

9_CD ._. 4_CD

9_CD ._. 4_CD ._. 1_LS ROLE_NNP OF_IN THE_DT STATISTICIAN_NNP
9_CD ._. 4_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 1_CD The_DT use_NN of_IN the_DT statistical_JJ methods_NNS described_VBD in_IN this_DT
manual_JJ for_IN routine_JJ data_NNS analysis_NN does_VBZ not_RB require_VB the_DT assistance_NN of_IN

this_DT manual_JJ can_MD become_VB problematic_JJ because_IN of_IN the_DT inherent_JJ

9_CD ._. 4_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 2_CD
The_DT statistical_JJ methods_NNS recommended_VBD in_IN this_DT manual_JJ are_VBP

methods_NNS have_VBP been_VBN proposed_VBN and_CC considered_VBN ._. Certainly_RB there_EX are_VBP

The_DT Wilcoxon_NNP Rank_NNP Sum_NNP Test_NNP is_VBZ a_DT nonparametric_JJ test_NN for_IN
comparing_VBG a_DT treatment_NN with_IN a_DT control_NN ._. The_DT data_NNS are_VBP ranked_VBN and_CC the_DT
analysis_NN proceeds_NNS exactly_RB as_IN in_IN Steel_NNP 's_POS Test_NNP except_IN that_DT
Bonferroni_NNP 's_POS adjustment_NN for_IN multiple_JJ comparisons_NNS is_VBZ used_VBN instead_RB of_IN
Steel_NNP 's_POS tables_NNS ._. When_WRB Steel_NNP 's_POS test_NN can_MD be_VB used_VBN (_( i_NNP ._. e_SYM ._. ,_, when_WRB there_EX are_VBP
equal_JJ numbers_NNS of_IN data_NNS points_NNS per_IN toxicant_NN concentration_NN )_) ,_, it_PRP will_MD
be_VB more_RBR powerful_JJ (_( able_JJ to_TO detect_VB smaller_JJR differences_NNS as_RB
statistically_RB significant_JJ )_) than_IN the_DT Wilcoxon_NNP Rank_NNP Sum_NNP Test_NNP with_IN
Bonferroni_NNP 's_POS adjustment_NN ._.


9_CD ._. 6_CD ._. 4_LS ._. 2_CD
The_DT estimate_NN of_IN the_DT safe_JJ concentration_NN is_VBZ reported_VBN as_IN the_DT
NOEC_NNP ._. A_DT step-by-step_JJ example_NN of_IN the_DT use_NN of_IN the_DT Wilcoxon_NNP Rank_NNP Sum_NNP
Test_NNP with_IN Bonferroni_NNP adjustment_NN is_VBZ provided_VBN in_IN Appendix_NNP
F_NNP ._.

9_CD ._. 7_CD

9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 1_LS PROBIT_NNP ANALYSIS_NNP


9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 1_CD
Probit_NNP Analysis_NNP is_VBZ used_VBN to_TO estimate_VB an_DT LC_NNP 1_CD ,_, LC_NNP 50_CD ,_, EC_NNP 1_CD ,_, or_CC
EC_NNP 50_CD and_CC the_DT associated_VBN 95_CD %_NN confidence_NN interval_NN ._. The_DT analysis_NN
consists_VBZ of_IN adjusting_VBG the_DT data_NNS for_IN mortality_NN in_IN the_DT control_NN ,_, and_CC
then_RB using_VBG a_DT maximum_NN likelihood_NN technique_NN to_TO estimate_VB the_DT
parameters_NNS of_IN the_DT underlying_VBG log_NN tolerance_NN distribution_NN ,_, which_WDT is_VBZ
assumed_VBN to_TO have_VB a_DT particular_JJ shape_NN ._.


9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 2_CD
The_DT assumption_NN upon_IN which_WDT the_DT use_NN of_IN Probit_NNP Analysis_NNP is_VBZ
contingent_NN is_VBZ a_DT normal_JJ distribution_NN of_IN log_NN tolerances_NNS ._. If_IN the_DT
normality_NN assumption_NN is_VBZ not_RB met_VBN ,_, and_CC at_IN least_JJS two_CD partial_JJ
mortalities_NNS are_VBP not_RB obtained_VBN ,_, Probit_NNP Analysis_NNP should_MD not_RB be_VB used_VBN ._.
It_PRP is_VBZ important_JJ to_TO check_VB the_DT results_NNS of_IN Probit_NNP Analysis_NNP to_TO
determine_VB if_IN use_NN of_IN the_DT analysis_NN is_VBZ appropriate_JJ ._. The_DT chi-square_JJ
test_NN for_IN heterogeneity_NN provides_VBZ a_DT good_JJ test_NN of_IN appropriateness_NN of_IN
the_DT analysis_NN ._. The_DT computer_NN program_NN (_( see_VB discussion_NN ,_, Appendix_NNP H_NNP )_)
checks_VBZ the_DT chi-square_JJ statistic_NN calculated_VBN for_IN the_DT data_NNS set_VBN against_IN
the_DT tabular_NN value_NN ,_, and_CC provides_VBZ an_DT error_NN message_NN if_IN the_DT calculated_VBN
value_NN exceeds_VBZ the_DT tabular_NN value_NN ._.


9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 3_CD
A_DT discussion_NN of_IN Probit_NNP Analysis_NNP ,_, and_CC examples_NNS of_IN computer_NN
program_NN input_NN and_CC output_NN ,_, are_VBP found_VBN in_IN Appendix_NNP H_NNP ._.


9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 1_LS ._. 4_CD
In_IN cases_NNS where_WRB Probit_NNP Analysis_NNP is_VBZ not_RB appropriate_JJ ,_, the_DT

9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 2_LS ._. 1_CD
The_DT Linear_NNP Interpolation_NNP Method_NNP (_( see_VB Appendix_NNP L_NNP )_) is_VBZ a_DT
procedure_NN to_TO calculate_VB a_DT point_NN estimate_NN of_IN the_DT effluent_JJ or_CC other_JJ
toxicant_NN concentration_NN [_NN Inhibition_NNP Concentration_NNP ,_, (_( IC_NNP )_) ]_NN that_IN causes_VBZ
a_DT given_VBN percent_NN reduction_NN (_( e_SYM ._. g_SYM ._. ,_, 25_CD %_NN ,_, 50_CD %_NN ,_, etc_FW ._. )_) in_IN the_DT
reproduction_NN ,_, growth_NN ,_, fertilization_NN ,_, or_CC fecundity_NN of_IN the_DT test_NN

the_DT analysis_NN of_IN data_NNS from_IN short-term_JJ chronic_JJ toxicity_NN
tests_NNS ._.


9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 2_LS ._. 2_CD
Use_NN of_IN the_DT Linear_NNP Interpolation_NNP Method_NNP is_VBZ based_VBN on_IN the_DT
assumptions_NNS that_IN the_DT responses_NNS (_( 1_LS )_) are_VBP monotonically_RB non-increasing_JJ
(_( the_DT mean_JJ response_NN for_IN each_DT higher_JJR concentration_NN is_VBZ less_JJR than_IN or_CC
equal_JJ to_TO the_DT mean_JJ response_NN for_IN the_DT previous_JJ concentration_NN )_) ,_, (_( 2_LS )_)
follow_VB a_DT piece-wise_JJ linear_JJ response_NN function_NN ,_, and_CC (_( 3_LS )_) are_VBP from_IN a_DT
random_JJ ,_, independent_JJ ,_, and_CC representative_NN sample_NN of_IN test_NN data_NNS ._. The_DT
assumption_NN for_IN piece-wise_JJ linear_JJ response_NN cannot_NN be_VB tested_VBN
statistically_RB ,_, and_CC no_DT defined_VBN statistical_JJ procedure_NN is_VBZ provided_VBN to_TO
test_VB the_DT assumption_NN for_IN monotonicity_NN ._. Where_WRB the_DT observed_VBD means_NNS are_VBP
not_RB strictly_RB monotonic_JJ by_IN examination_NN ,_, they_PRP are_VBP adjusted_VBN by_IN
smoothing_VBG ._. In_IN cases_NNS where_WRB the_DT responses_NNS at_IN the_DT low_JJ toxicant_NN
concentrations_NNS are_VBP much_RB higher_JJR than_IN in_IN the_DT controls_NNS ,_, the_DT smoothing_VBG
process_NN may_MD result_VB in_IN a_DT large_JJ upward_RB adjustment_NN in_IN the_DT control_NN

9_CD ._. 7_CD ._. 2_LS ._. 3_CD
The_DT inability_NN to_TO test_VB the_DT monotonicity_NN and_CC piece_VB wise_JJ
linear_JJ response_NN assumptions_NNS for_IN this_DT method_NN makes_VBZ it_PRP difficult_JJ to_TO
assess_VB when_WRB the_DT method_NN is_VBZ ,_, or_CC is_VBZ not_RB ,_, producing_VBG reliable_JJ results_NNS ._.
Therefore_RB ,_, the_DT method_NN should_MD be_VB used_VBN with_IN caution_NN when_WRB the_DT results_NNS

concentration_NN to_TO the_DT next_JJ in_IN the_DT concentration_NN series_NN ,_, and_CC when_WRB it_PRP
appears_VBZ that_IN there_EX is_VBZ a_DT large_JJ deviation_NN from_IN monotonicity_NN ._. See_VB

10_CD ._. 2_LS ._. 6_CD CONCENTRATION-RESPONSE_NNP RELATIONSHIPS_NNP


10_CD ._. 2_LS ._. 6_CD ._. 1_LS
The_DT concept_NN of_IN a_DT concentration-response_JJ ,_, or_CC more_RBR
classically_RB ,_, a_DT dose-response_JJ relationship_NN is_VBZ "_'' the_DT most_RBS fundamental_JJ
